I went to the site and learned that its only there to give girth. apparently without it you don't get that full lash look that buyers wanted so they added the white step. its not necessary for the \\"tubing\\" process.<br /><br />then do the same with the mascara itself- really scrape off excess from the applicator. and work one eye at a time to declump before drying.
